# New objects

5
141
""Diplomat's Cloak
In addition to component effect this cloak allows your hero to retreat or surrender when battling neutral monsters or defending a város as well as when attacking and casting a spell in the first round of a combat. It also multiplies your hero army strength by 3 (for neutral armies and Thieves guild).
Requires the following Mûtárgyak to create:
+Statesman's Medal
+Diplomat's Ring
+Ambassador's Sash""

5
142
""Pendant of Reflection
In addition to component effect this item increases your chance to resist a hostile spell by 20%.
Requires the following Mûtárgyak to create:
+Garniture of Interference
+Surcoat of Counterpoise
+Boots of Polarity""

5
143
""Ironfist of the Ogre
In addition to component effect the Ironfist of the Ogre casts these spells on expert level at the beginning of combat on all of your creatures for fifty rounds: Haste, Bloodlust, Fire Shield, and Counterstrike.
Requires the following Mûtárgyak to create:
+Crown of the Supreme Magi
+Ogre's Club of Havoc
+Tunic of the Cyclops King
+Targ of the Rampaging Ogre""

5
161
""Horn of the Abyss
Osztály: Ereklye.
After a stack of living creatures is slain, a stack of Polipfej will rise in their stead and will stay loyal to the hero after the battle concludes. Total Hit Points of this stack will be equal to half of the slain stack's total Hit Points, but mennyiség of the Polipfej summoned thus should not exceed half of mennyiség of creatures in the slain stack. Slaying Polipfej will not trigger the Horn effect.""
